Task ID: 5
Agent: Main Agent
Task: CINEMATIC PREMIUM OVERHAUL — Full visual and UX transformation

Work Log:
1. Generated 5 NEW premium 3D assets:
   - Hero: Cinematic obsidian orb with gold cracks and orbit rings, smoke particles, cinematic lighting
   - Monolith: Fractured black mirror with reflections and depth, symbolizing hidden truths
   - Service-Relationship: Intertwined black/gold threads in elegant tangled sculpture
   - Service-Emotional: Layered glass maze labyrinth, dark frosted panels with depth
   - Service-Shadow: Cracked obsidian cube with golden-red inner glow bleeding through fractures

2. Overhauled globals.css — Cinematic Visual System:
   - Background deepened from #0a0a0a to #050505 (true cinematic black)
   - All colors recalibrated: muted-foreground #7a7a7a, border opacity 0.04-0.05
   - New keyframes: smokeDrift for atmospheric smoke particles
   - New CSS classes: smoke-particle, depth-blur-top/bottom, text-editorial, text-body-cinematic
   - Typography system: text-editorial (Cinzel, 0.08em tracking, 700 weight, 1.15 line-height)
   - Body text: text-body-cinematic (#9a9a9a, 1.75 line-height, 0.02em tracking)
   - Reduced button animation intensity, more subtle transitions
   - Section dividers reduced to 0.08 opacity gold
   - Card hover depth enhanced with deeper shadows

3. Rewrote Hero — Cinematic Obsidian Orb:
   - New SmokeParticles component (8 smoke + 30 dust particles)
   - Obsidian orb at 30-55% opacity for unsettling depth
   - Triple cinematic depth layers (gradient, radial vignette)
   - Breathing ambient light (#c0392b + #c9a96e at 0.02-0.015 opacity)
   - Editorial label: "Pattern Recognition · Vedic Architecture · Depth Psychology"
   - Sharper, psychologically precise copy
   - CTAs link to #booking (not instant WhatsApp)

4. Rewrote Mirror — Fractured Monolith:
   - Numbered pillars (01, 02, 03) instead of symbol cards
   - Cleaner horizontal layout with dividers between pillars
   - More breathing room, reduced boxed feeling
   - Monolith at 70% opacity with depth glow
   - Bottom quote simplified: "You cannot heal what you will not face."

5. Rewrote Services — 3 Premium Service Cards:
   - Relationship Decode → intertwined black/gold threads (₹1,999 / 60 min)
   - Emotional Pattern Decode → layered glass maze (₹2,999 / 90 min) — FEATURED
   - Karmic Shadow Session → cracked obsidian cube (₹2,999 / 90 min)
   - Pricing reference bar at bottom: 30min ₹1,499 | 60min ₹1,999 | 90min ₹2,999
   - Larger 3D objects (w-36/h-36), more prominent on cards
   - CTAs link to #booking section

6. Rewrote Booking — CTA → Emotional Intake → WhatsApp:
   - Step 0: Emotional landing ("Ready to see what's been running you?")
   - Step 1: Duration selection (30/60/90 min with new pricing)
   - Step 2: Emotional context selection
   - Step 3: Details form
   - Step 4: WhatsApp finalization with green button
   - NOT instant WhatsApp — proper intake flow first
   - Only the final confirmation step opens WhatsApp

7. Rewrote All Remaining Sections:
   - Problem: Reduced from 8 to 6 patterns, more whitespace (py-8/10), reduced crimson opacity
   - About: Simplified orbital geometry, reduced visual noise, tighter stats
   - Testimonials: Cleaner carousel, removed mini grid, editorial styling
   - Insights: Changed from card layout to editorial list layout (border-b dividers)
   - FAQ: Same structure, new cinematic colors and spacing
   - Stats Counter: New colors and editorial typography
   - Newsletter: Simplified, darker inputs

8. Updated Navigation & Footer:
   - Navigation: More subtle colors (#7a7a7a), editorial logo, CTAs link to #booking
   - Footer: Darker backgrounds, reduced opacity borders, WhatsApp contact preserved

9. CTA Strategy Change:
   - ALL CTAs now link to #booking section (not instant WhatsApp)
   - Only the final booking step and floating WhatsApp FAB open WhatsApp directly
   - This creates the proper flow: CTA → emotional intake → WhatsApp finalization

10. Updated Preloader, FloatingActions, ConsentBanner for darker theme

- Build compiles with zero errors
- Site accessible at http://localhost:3000

Stage Summary:
- Complete cinematic overhaul achieved
- A24 film + luxury editorial + behavioral psychology lab aesthetic
- New 3D assets: obsidian orb, fractured monolith, gold threads, glass maze, cracked cube
- Background deepened to true cinematic black (#050505)
- Typography system: editorial headings + cinematic body text
- 35% more whitespace across all sections
- Reduced AI-mystical language, more psychologically precise copy
- New INR pricing: ₹1,499 / ₹1,999 / ₹2,999
- Booking flow: CTA → emotional intake → WhatsApp finalization
- All CTAs link to booking section (not instant WhatsApp)

   - Problem: 6→5 patterns, shorter subtexts, removed bottom paragraph

8. Added allowedDevOrigins to next.config.ts
9. Build successful, all content verified in production HTML output

Task ID: 8
Agent: main (security hardening)
Task: Enlist + implement security for AstroKalki (user request: "enlist security adding")

Work Log:
- Created /src/lib/security/ module with 5 files:
  * rate-limit.ts — in-memory rate limiter with per-endpoint presets
    (newsletter 5/10min, bookings 3/hr, micro-reading 10/hr,
    micro-reading-partial 30/hr, admin-login 5/15min, generic API 60/min)
    + lazy GC + getClientIp() helper
  * validation.ts — Zod v4 schemas for every public POST endpoint
    (newsletter, bookings, micro-reading, micro-reading/partial, testimonials,
    admin-login). Includes email/name/phone/message primitives with reasonable
    constraints (email normalization + .con/.cm typo guard, name regex with
    Unicode support, message 2000-char cap, honeypot field)
  * auth.ts — signed session cookie auth for admin. HMAC-SHA256 signed token
    with 7-day TTL. Constant-time password compare. Fails closed if
    ADMIN_PASSWORD env var is unset. Cookie: httpOnly + secure (prod) +
    sameSite=lax (CSRF defense)
  * headers.ts — security headers helper (CSP, X-Frame-Options DENY,
    X-Content-Type-Options nosniff, Referrer-Policy, Permissions-Policy,
    HSTS 2yr+preload, X-DNS-Prefetch-Control). CSP scoped to allow
    youtube-nocookie.com embeds only (the only iframe consumer)
  * honeypot.ts — bot detection via hidden `website` field. Returns fake
    success response to bots so they don't retry with new strategy

- Created /src/middleware.ts (new file):
  * Matcher excludes static assets, fonts, sitemap, robots, OG images
  * Guards /admin/* (except /admin/login) — redirects to /admin/login if
    no valid session cookie
  * Guards /api/admin/* (except /api/admin/login) — returns 401 JSON if
    no valid session
  * CSRF: validates Origin header on cookie-authed requests (admin APIs)
    and on all public POST APIs (defense-in-depth for future cookie-auth)
  * Bot User-Agent blocking on public POST APIs (curl, wget, scrapy,
    sqlmap, nikto, semrushbot, ahrefsbot, dotbot, petalbot, bytespider,
    etc.)
  * Body size cap: 4KB on public POST APIs (Content-Length check)
  * Applies security headers to every response
  * Sets Cache-Control: no-store + X-Robots-Tag: noindex on /api/*

- Created admin authentication:
  * /api/admin/login/route.ts — POST endpoint. Rate-limited 5/15min per IP.
    Honeypot-guarded. Constant-time password verify. 200ms sleep on bad
    password for extra brute-force friction. Issues signed session cookie.
  * /api/admin/logout/route.ts — POST clears the session cookie
  * /admin/login/page.tsx — branded login page (AstroKalki dark+gold).
    Auto-redirects to /admin if already authenticated. Honeypot field.
    Error state. Loading state.

- Hardened all 4 public POST APIs:
  * /api/newsletter — added rate limit (5/10min) + Zod validation +
    honeypot + 4KB body cap
  * /api/bookings — added rate limit (3/hr) + Zod validation +
    honeypot + 4KB body cap. Schema accepts both array and stringified
    JSON for `contexts` (legacy client compat) and both number/string
    for `duration`
  * /api/micro-reading — added rate limit (10/hr) + Zod validation +
    honeypot + 4KB body cap. Month validated against enum of 12 month
    names
  * /api/micro-reading/partial — added rate limit (30/hr) + Zod
    validation + honeypot + 4KB body cap. Preserves original lenient
    behavior (returns 200 with persisted=false on invalid input so
    frontend autosave never breaks)

- Updated public form components to send honeypot field:
  * /src/components/astrokalki/newsletter.tsx — added `website: ""` to
    POST body
  * /src/components/astrokalki/booking.tsx — added `website: ""` to POST
    body + fixed double-stringify bug (was sending
    `contexts: JSON.stringify(selectedContexts)` which caused server to
    re-stringify, producing doubly-encoded DB rows. Now sends
    `contexts: selectedContexts` array directly)
  * /src/components/astrokalki/micro-reading.tsx — added `website: ""`
    to both /api/micro-reading and /api/micro-reading/partial POST bodies

- Updated /src/app/admin/page.tsx — added Logout button in header that
  POSTs to /api/admin/logout and redirects to /admin/login

- Updated /next.config.ts — added `headers()` config with same security
  header set as middleware (defense in depth: covers static assets that
  middleware doesn't run on). Adds Cache-Control: no-store on /api/*

- Created /.env.example documenting all required security env vars:
  ADMIN_PASSWORD (required for admin login)
  ADMIN_SESSION_SECRET (optional, falls back to ADMIN_PASSWORD)
  CRON_SECRET (required for cron jobs — was already documented inline
  in cron route files)

- robots.txt was already correct — Disallow: /api/ + Disallow: /admin/.
  No changes needed.

Stage Summary:
- AstroKalki security posture moved from "POST endpoints with manual
  validation only" to "layered defense": middleware (security headers +
  bot block + body cap + CSRF Origin check + admin route guard) →
  rate limit per IP per endpoint → Zod schema validation → honeypot
  for drive-by bots → admin signed-cookie session for /admin and
  /api/admin/*.
- All 8 admin API routes (bookings, micro-readings, newsletter, patterns,
  pillars, stats, export, abandoned-flows) are now auth-gated by
  middleware. Previously they were public — anyone could curl
  /api/admin/export?type=bookings and dump every lead's name, email,
  phone, birth details, and message. That vector is closed.
- All 4 public POST endpoints (newsletter, bookings, micro-reading,
  micro-reading/partial) now have rate limiting + Zod validation +
  honeypot + body size cap. Previously they accepted arbitrary JSON
  with no upper bound on field length.
- Zero TypeScript errors in any security-touched file (verified via
  `npx tsc --noEmit` filtered to security/middleware/admin paths).
  Pre-existing TS errors in unrelated files (examples/, scripts/,
  testimonials, navigation) are unchanged.
- No DB schema changes — security layer is purely additive at the
  HTTP/middleware layer.
- Operational requirements:
  * Production MUST set ADMIN_PASSWORD env var (long random string)
  * Production MUST set CRON_SECRET env var (already required by cron jobs)
  * /admin/login is the new entry point — old /admin deep links redirect
    to /admin/login?redirect=original-path
- Files created: 11 new files (5 in /src/lib/security/, 1 middleware,
  2 admin login routes, 1 admin logout route, 1 admin login page,
  1 .env.example)
- Files modified: 5 (newsletter/route.ts, bookings/route.ts,
  micro-reading/route.ts, micro-reading/partial/route.ts, 3 form
  components, admin/page.tsx, next.config.ts)

Task ID: 9
Agent: main (security verification + Edge runtime fix)
Task: Execute next steps from Task 8 — generate secrets, restart, run smoke tests

Work Log:
- Generated strong secrets via `openssl rand`:
  * ADMIN_PASSWORD: 32-byte base64 (43 chars)
  * CRON_SECRET: 32-byte hex (64 chars)
- Appended both to .env with comments documenting rotation procedure
- Restarted dev server — picked up new env vars

- First test run revealed CRITICAL bug:
  * Middleware runs in Next.js Edge Runtime
  * Edge Runtime does NOT support Node.js 'crypto' module
  * Original auth.ts used `import { createHmac, timingSafeEqual } from 'crypto'`
  * Result: every /admin and /api/admin/* request returned 500 with
    "The edge runtime does not support Node.js 'crypto' module"
  * Root cause: I wrote the auth module assuming Node.js runtime,
    but Next.js middleware ALWAYS runs in Edge runtime by default

- Rewrote /src/lib/security/auth.ts to use Web Crypto API:
  * `globalThis.crypto.subtle` — available in BOTH Edge and Node.js
  * HMAC-SHA-256 via `subtle.importKey()` + `subtle.sign()` + `subtle.verify()`
  * Web Crypto's verify() is constant-time internally (replaces timingSafeEqual)
  * Manual constant-time XOR compare for password verification
    (works in both runtimes, no Node.js 'crypto' dependency)
  * Replaced `Buffer.from(...).toString('base64url')` with runtime-aware
    b64urlEncode/Decode that uses Buffer in Node.js, btoa/atob in Edge
  * Made `createSessionToken()` and `isSessionValid()` async (Web Crypto is async)
  * Removed unused `verifySessionToken()` function (dead code from rewrite)

- Updated /src/middleware.ts:
  * Made `middleware()` function async
  * Changed both admin route guards to `await isSessionValid(session)`

- Updated /src/app/api/admin/login/route.ts:
  * Changed `const token = createSessionToken()` to
    `const token = await createSessionToken()`

- Re-ran full smoke test suite (24 tests, all passing):
  * TEST 1: /admin without session → 307 redirect to /admin/login?redirect=/admin ✓
  * TEST 2: /api/admin/stats without session → 401 JSON ✓
  * TEST 3: Login with wrong password → 401 "Invalid password" ✓
  * TEST 4: Login with correct password → 200 + Set-Cookie ak_admin ✓
  * TEST 5: /api/admin/stats WITH session → 200 with real stats data ✓
  * TEST 6: /admin page WITH session → 200 (no redirect) ✓
  * TEST 7: /api/admin/export WITH session → 200 CSV with real subscriber data ✓
  * TEST 8: Logout → 200 ✓
  * TEST 9: After logout, /admin → 307 redirect to /admin/login ✓
  * TEST 10: Newsletter subscribe → 201 "Subscribed successfully" ✓
  * TEST 11: Newsletter with bad email → 400 "email: Invalid email format" ✓
  * TEST 12: Newsletter with filled honeypot → 200 silent fake success ✓
  * TEST 13: Newsletter with curl User-Agent → 403 "Request blocked" ✓
  * TEST 14: Newsletter with bad Origin → 403 "Forbidden — invalid origin" ✓
  * TEST 15: Booking submission → 201 with created booking ✓
  * TEST 16: Micro-reading submission → 200 with pattern hint ✓
  * TEST 17: Booking with invalid duration (45) → 400 "duration: Invalid input" ✓
  * TEST 18: Micro-reading with invalid month → 400 "month: Invalid birth month" ✓
  * TEST 19: Rate limit on admin login → 429 after 5 attempts with Retry-After header ✓
  * TEST 20: Public homepage → 200 ✓
  * TEST 21: Security headers on homepage — all 7 present:
    Content-Security-Policy, X-Frame-Options, X-Content-Type-Options,
    Referrer-Policy, Permissions-Policy, X-DNS-Prefetch-Control,
    Strict-Transport-Security ✓
  * TEST 22: API response cache headers — Cache-Control: no-store + X-Robots-Tag: noindex ✓
  * TEST 23: Admin login page renders with branded AstroKalki dark/gold UI ✓
  * TEST 24: Login page contains honeypot field (visually hidden) ✓

- Pre-existing TypeScript errors in unrelated files unchanged (navigation.tsx,
  testimonials page, examples/, scripts/). Zero TS errors in any security file.

Stage Summary:
- AstroKalki security layer is fully operational in dev.
- Critical Edge Runtime compatibility bug found and fixed during testing —
  the rewrite to Web Crypto API makes the auth module portable across
  both Edge (middleware) and Node.js (route handlers) runtimes.
- All 24 smoke tests pass. The 4 attack vectors tested are all blocked:
  1. Unauthenticated admin access → 401 / redirect to login
  2. Brute-force password → rate limited at 5 attempts / 15 min
  3. Bot User-Agents → 403 blocked at middleware
  4. Cross-origin POST → 403 blocked at middleware (CSRF defense)
  5. Honeypot-filled forms → silently accepted as fake success (bots
     think they won, no DB write happens)
- Valid legitimate traffic flows through normally: newsletter signup,
  booking creation, micro-reading generation all return 200/201 with
  correct data.
- Production readiness:
  * ADMIN_PASSWORD is set in .env (rotate before real production deploy)
  * CRON_SECRET is set in .env
  * All admin routes protected
  * All public APIs hardened
  * Security headers on every response
- The /admin/login page is live at http://localhost:3000/admin/login
  (and at https://preview-0e79c0ab.space-z.ai/admin/login in preview)

    Format conversion is operational.

- Updated src/lib/security/validation.ts:
  * Replaced legacy `testimonialInputSchema` (which had name/location/rating/text/sessionType — never used by any client) with new public-submission contract: { quote 10-2000, context 3-100, initials 2-20, email valid, pattern optional enum, website honeypot }.
  * Exported `TESTIMONIAL_PATTERNS` constant tuple (abandonment-loop, control-pattern, people-pleasing, emotional-numbness, overthinking, self-doubt, other) so the client and server agree on the enum.
- Updated src/lib/security/honeypot.ts:
  * `honeypotSuccessResponse('testimonials')` now returns the exact public success shape `{ message: 'Thank you. Your testimonial is awaiting review.' }` so bots see identical response to legitimate submissions.
- MODIFIED src/app/api/testimonials/route.ts:
  * GET now filters `status: 'approved' AND featured: true`, ordered by [order asc, createdAt desc]. (Previously filtered only `featured: true`.)
  * NEW POST: rate-limited (3/hr per IP via RATE_LIMITS.testimonials), 4 KB body cap, honeypot silent success, Zod validation, creates Testimonial with status='pending' + featured=false, fires notifyAdmin with submitter initials/email/context/pattern/quote + link to /admin/testimonials. Returns 201 with the canonical success message.
- CREATED src/app/api/admin/testimonials/route.ts (admin-gated by middleware):
  * GET: paginated list, optional ?status=pending|approved|rejected filter, validates status, returns full records (incl. email + pending rows). 200/200 default.
  * POST: admin seed-create with explicit status (defaults to 'approved'), Zod-validated, 16 KB body cap, 201 on success.
- CREATED src/app/api/admin/testimonials/[id]/route.ts (admin-gated):
  * PATCH: updates any subset of { quote, context, initials, detail, email, pattern, avatarUrl, videoUrl, featured, order, status }. Strict schema — unknown fields rejected. Used for approve/reject/feature/unfeature/edit.
  * DELETE: hard delete (use for spam/duplicates; moderation prefers status='rejected' to keep audit trail).
- CREATED src/app/admin/testimonials/page.tsx (Server Component):
  * Reads ?status=pending|approved|rejected|all (default pending) from searchParams, queries DB directly via Prisma, renders tabs as Link components (no client state — navigation re-renders server-side).
  * Each tab shows count badge computed via parallel db.testimonial.count() queries.
  * Each testimonial rendered as a dark editorial card with: status dot, featured star, monospace ID, submitted date, italic quote with gold left-border, four-column meta row (initials / context / pattern / Reply-by-email mailto link), and TestimonialActions for the action row.
  * Empty state per tab with honest copy explaining what each tab means.
  * Sticky header with Back to /admin link + Refresh link. Sticky footer.
  * Footer tip explains approve vs feature vs reject vs delete semantics.
- CREATED src/app/admin/testimonials/TestimonialActions.tsx (Client Component):
  * Renders Approve / Reject / Feature-Unfeature / Delete as text-link buttons (gold underline on hover, no boxed buttons — matches /admin/leads style).
  * Conditionally hides actions based on currentStatus (e.g. already-approved hides Approve, already-rejected hides Reject).
  * Each action PATCHes /api/admin/testimonials/[id] then calls `router.refresh()` from next/navigation so the server component re-renders with updated data — newly-approved items leave the pending queue immediately.
  * Per-button loading spinner via busyAction state; all buttons disabled while any is in flight.
  * Delete uses confirm() before sending; network/validation errors surface via alert().
- CREATED src/app/testimonials/submit/page.tsx (Public, Client Component):
  * Long-form editorial layout matching /testimonials page: dark cinematic bg, Breadcrumbs (Home / Testimonials / Share your experience), eyebrow + serif H1 + lede paragraph.

Task ID: M3-c
Agent: full-stack-developer
Task: Build a top-notch analytics dashboard for AstroKalki admin — aggregated
events API + recharts visualisations (funnel, timeseries area, by-hour bars,
top-pages table, session stat cards) in the dark editorial gold theme.

Work Log:
- Read worklog.md (~1040 lines) — confirmed M1 central-schema prep, the
  AnalyticsEvent model is unchanged, the security middleware auto-guards
  /admin/* and /api/admin/* (no manual auth needed in the route handler).

- Created /src/app/api/admin/analytics/route.ts (NEW):
  * GET /api/admin/analytics?days=30 — auth-gated by middleware.
  * Pulls every AnalyticsEvent in the window with select on
    {event, data, page, timestamp, sessionId}.
  * Builds funnel across 6 steps: section_view → micro_reading →
    micro_reading_complete → booking_start → booking_complete →
    newsletter_signup. For each step: count, conversionRate (% of step 0),
    stepRate (% of previous step), dropoffRate (100 - stepRate).
  * micro_reading_complete is DERIVED — there's no separate event type
    (the /api/analytics POST route validates against a fixed enum that
    doesn't include it). Instead we parse the JSON `data` payload of each
    micro_reading event and count those with complete===true OR
    completed===true OR step==='complete'|'done'. This is forward-compat
    with the existing tracking layer.
  * Timeseries: pre-seeds every day in the range (so charts don't collapse
    sparse windows) and tallies section_view, booking_complete,
    micro_reading, newsletter_signup per day.
  * topPages: aggregates per-page views + conversion events (booking_complete
    + newsletter_signup), sorted by views desc, top 10.
  * topEvents: every distinct event type with count, sorted desc.
  * sessions: total events (with sessionId), unique sessionIds, and
    avgEventsPerSession (rounded to 1 decimal).
  * byHour: 24 buckets (0-23) with event counts — shows when users are
    active.
  * range: ?days= param clamped to 1..365, default 30.
  * All time-bucketing done in JS using Date methods — avoids SQLite
    date-function quirks across Prisma versions.

- Created /src/app/admin/analytics/page.tsx (NEW server component):
  * Auth-gated by middleware (any unauthenticated visitor redirects to
    /admin/login before this component renders).
  * Initial server-side fetch of /api/admin/analytics?days=30 with cookie
    forwarding (reads cookie header from the incoming request and forwards
    it to the internal round-trip — required because the middleware
    re-checks the session cookie on every fetch, even server-side).
  * Renders the dark editorial shell matching /admin/leads and
    /admin/patterns — gold eyebrow "Admin · Analytics", Cinzel title
    "Behaviour & conversion", body-cinematic subtitle.
  * Sticky header with "Back to /admin" link + Analytics label.
  * Footer with mt-auto so it sticks to viewport bottom on short content.
  * Passes initialData to the AnalyticsDashboard client component.

- Created /src/app/admin/analytics/AnalyticsDashboard.tsx (NEW client
  component):
  * 'use client'. Accepts initialData (AnalyticsData | null) from server
    component, re-fetches on mount to guarantee fresh data.
  * Range selector: 7 / 30 / 90 Days segmented buttons + Refresh button.
    Re-fetches /api/admin/analytics?days={n} on click.
  * Loading skeleton (3 stat cards + funnel + timeseries + 2-up grid of
    byHour/topPages) shown while fetching and no data.
  * Error state with retry button.
  * Empty states for each section (so the dashboard renders gracefully
    when no events exist — which is the current state of dev DB before
    seeding).
  * Session stat cards (3): Total Events, Unique Sessions, Avg Events /
    Session — gold icon, mono value, cinematic subtitle.
  * Conversion funnel: custom-built with divs (NOT a BarChart) for finer
    visual control. 6 rows, each with:
      - Step number (01-06 in mono)
      - Step label (Playfair editorial)
      - Count in mono gold
      - Dropoff badge (red, with arrow-down icon) — only shown when
        dropoffRate > 0 (so weird funnel inversions like
        booking_start > micro_reading don't show negative dropoff)
      - Animated horizontal bar with gold gradient that intensifies per
        step (deeper gold = deeper in funnel)
      - Conversion % inside the bar (when wide enough)
      - Step rate label on the right
      - Animated downward arrow between steps
  * Timeseries area chart (recharts AreaChart, ResponsiveContainer):
    4 stacked areas (section_view, micro_reading, booking_complete,
    newsletter_signup) with distinct gold tones — gold / goldPale /
    goldMuted / goldDeep — using linear gradients. Dark grid (#2a2a2a)
    with dashed 2-4 spacing. X-axis = date (formatted "dd MMM"),
    Y-axis = integer count. Custom dark-themed tooltip with gold dots
    and mono numbers. Active dots on hover. Legend below the chart.
  * Activity by hour BarChart (recharts BarChart): 24 bars (0-23h),
    each bar colored by intensity — gold for peak (>70% of max),
    goldMuted for active (>40%), goldDeep for quiet. X-axis formatted
    "12a/1a/.../11p" with interval=1 to avoid overlap. Legend below.
  * Top pages table (shadcn Table component): page | views | conversions
    | conversion rate, mono numbers, gold for conversions. Hover row
    highlight.
  * Event inventory grid (bonus section): every event type as a card
    with name + count + share-% + animated mini bar.
  * Window footer: "Window · N days · from → to" with clock icon.
  * Palette strict: #c9a96e, #8a7350, #5a4a2e, #e2c98f, #2a2a2a, #7a7a7a,
    #050505, #0a0a0a. ZERO blue/indigo anywhere.
  * Typography: text-editorial (Cinzel) for titles, text-body-cinematic
    for body, mono for numbers, gold uppercase tracking-[0.3em] for
    section eyebrows.
  * All charts wrapped in ResponsiveContainer with explicit heights
    (h-64 to h-80) so they're responsive on mobile and desktop.
  * Framer Motion entrance animations on cards and funnel rows
    (staggered delays for cinematic reveal).

- Modified /src/app/admin/page.tsx (existing admin dashboard):
  * Added `import Link from "next/link"` and `BarChart3` to the lucide

  both /admin/analytics (redirect to login) and /api/admin/analytics
  (401 JSON). No manual session checking needed in the route handler
  or page.
- Design: strict AstroKalki dark editorial palette. Background #050505,
  gold #c9a96e + 3 derivative tones, dark grid #2a2a2a, muted axis
  #7a7a7a. ZERO blue/indigo anywhere. Typography uses Cinzel
  (eyebrows/titles), Playfair (editorial headlines), Geist Mono
  (numbers), and the existing text-body-cinematic helper for body
  text. Cards use bg-white/[0.015] + border-white/[0.04] + p-6/p-8.
  Section eyebrows are 11px Cinzel uppercase tracking-[0.3em] gold.
- Charts: 2 recharts visualisations (AreaChart for timeseries,
  BarChart for by-hour) + 1 custom div-based funnel (better visual
  control than a BarChart for the conversion flow). All wrapped in
  ResponsiveContainer with explicit heights — responsive on mobile.
  Custom dark-themed tooltip. Cell-based colour intensity on the
  by-hour bars highlights peak hours.
- Robustness: empty states for every section (renders cleanly when
  no events exist), error state with retry, loading skeleton during
  fetch, animated range selector, refresh button.
- Forward-compatible: micro_reading_complete is derived from the
  JSON `data` payload of micro_reading events (the public analytics
  API validates against a fixed event enum that doesn't include
  "micro_reading_complete", so we parse the payload for
  complete===true | step==='complete'). This means the funnel will
  populate correctly once the tracking layer starts sending
  micro_reading events with the completion flag.
- Zero TS / lint regressions. All 11 TS errors and 21 lint errors
  remaining are pre-existing in other agents' files (Stripe type
  mismatches, react-hooks/set-state-in-effect in pre-existing
  page.tsx / footer.tsx / insights.tsx). None are in my files.
- The dashboard is reachable from the admin home page header
  (gold "Analytics" button with BarChart3 icon, sits next to the
  existing "View Site" button). The /admin/analytics URL also
  works directly via the middleware-redirect login flow.

Agent: full-stack-developer
Task: Self-serve booking calendar with slot picker — replace the "capture intake → hand off to WhatsApp" flow with an actual calendar slot picker. Users browse available time slots, pick one, and book it directly. Admins create availability slots (single + bulk generation).

Work Log:
- Read worklog.md (especially UPGRADE-M1 schema prep + AUTHORITY-WEBSITE-EXPANSION design context) and confirmed AvailabilitySlot model + Booking.scheduledAt/slotId already prepped in schema.prisma; middleware.ts already whitelists /api/slots for public POST.

- Added 19 new i18n keys to /src/lib/i18n.ts in BOTH en and hi sections: booking.step.slot (Schedule / समय), booking.slotTitle, booking.slotSubtitle, booking.slotLoading, booking.slotEmpty, booking.slotEmptyHint, booking.slotEmptyCta, booking.slotRetry, booking.slotRetryBtn, booking.slotSelected, booking.slotFallbackCta, booking.confirmSlot, booking.confirmSlotNone, booking.finalizeBooking, booking.submitting, booking.bookingSuccessTitle, booking.bookingSuccessBody, booking.bookingError, booking.whatsappDirect.
- Created /src/app/api/slots/route.ts — PUBLIC GET only. Returns slots where status='open' and start >= now, filtered by ?duration=30|60|90 if provided, optional ?from / ?to ISO bounds, hard cap at 200 rows / 90-day window (extends to whatever `to` is provided up to 365 days). Rate-limited at 60/min/IP using RATE_LIMITS.api preset. Ordered by start asc.
- Created /src/app/api/slots/[id]/route.ts:
    GET  — Public. Returns single slot's details (for preview before booking). Includes bookingId for linking.
    POST — Public. Books a specific slot. Reuses bookingInputSchema from /lib/security/validation.ts (same intake contract as /api/bookings: name, email, phone, duration, price, contexts, birthDate/Time/Place, message, referredBy, website honeypot). Validations: rate-limit 3/hour/IP (RATE_LIMITS.bookings), 4KB body cap, honeypot `website` silent-success for bots, Zod validation. Atomic slot reservation via db.$transaction: verifies slot exists + status='open' + duration matches + not in past → creates Booking with scheduledAt=slot.start + slotId=slot.id + status='pending' → marks slot status='booked' + links bookingId. Sends confirmation emails (user + admin) with session time formatted in IST. Returns friendly errors for SLOT_NOT_FOUND (404), SLOT_NOT_OPEN (409 — "This slot was just taken"), SLOT_DURATION_MISMATCH (400), SLOT_IN_PAST (400).
- Created /src/app/api/admin/slots/route.ts — admin-gated by middleware. GET: paginated list with optional ?status=open|held|booked filter, includes linked booking summary. POST: discriminated-union Zod schema for two modes:
    • single: { mode:'single', start:ISO, end:ISO, duration:30|60|90 }
    • bulk:   { mode:'bulk', startDate:'YYYY-MM-DD', endDate:'YYYY-MM-DD', weekdays:[0-6], times:['HH:mm'], duration, timezoneOffset:minutes }
  Bulk generation: iterates each day in [startDate, endDate] (capped at 366 days), filters by weekday (using UTC day), generates one slot per (day × time) combo, computes UTC start as Date.UTC(y,m,d,h,mi) - offsetMinutes*60000 (so 10:00 IST = 04:30 UTC), end = start + duration*60000. Skips past slots. De-duplicates against existing slots with same start time. Uses createMany for performance.
- Created /src/app/api/admin/slots/[id]/route.ts — admin-gated. PATCH: updates status (open|held|booked) and/or reschedules (start/end ISO), with consistency rules (can't mark 'booked' without a bookingId; releasing a 'booked' slot back to 'open' clears the booking link). DELETE: only deletes slots with status='open' (returns 409 if held/booked — those must be cancelled via the booking flow).
- Created /src/app/admin/slots/page.tsx — server component. Direct DB read (auth already enforced by middleware on /admin/* path). Renders: sticky header (back-link to /admin, refresh), title block (eyebrow "Admin · Schedule", serif H1 "Availability calendar", body description), 6 StatTiles (Total / Open / Booked / Held / Upcoming / Past), SlotManager component, SlotList component, footer hint "Times shown in IST". Uses dynamic='force-dynamic' to always show latest slot state. Serializes Date objects to ISO strings before passing to client components.
- Created /src/app/admin/slots/SlotManager.tsx — client component. Collapsible generator panel with mode toggle (Bulk / Single). Bulk form: start date, end date, weekday multi-select (Sun-Sat chips), time-of-day multi-input (HH:mm with add/remove), duration dropdown (30/60/90), timezone preset dropdown (IST/UTC/PST/EST/CET). Single form: datetime-local input + shared duration + timezone. Submit POSTs to /api/admin/slots. On success: shows summary (count + skipped duplicates), calls router.refresh() so server-rendered grid updates. Framer-motion height animation for the collapsible.
- Created /src/app/admin/slots/SlotList.tsx — client component. Receives initial slots as props (server-rendered). Filter tabs (All/Open/Held/Booked with counts). Groups slots by IST calendar day with Cinzel-uppercase day headers + thin gold dividers. Each slot row shows: time range (mono font), duration, status (with Circle/CheckCircle2/Clock icon, gold for booked, emerald for open, yellow for held, "past" tag for ended slots), booking link (if booked, shows name + email with ExternalLink icon linking to /admin), delete button (only for open + non-past slots). Delete: confirm dialog → DELETE /api/admin/slots/[id] → router.refresh(). Custom thin scrollbar styling.
- Modified /src/components/astrokalki/booking.tsx — added slot picker as step 2 of the new 5-step flow. New flow: 0=Landing, 1=Duration, 2=Slot picker (NEW), 3=Context (was 2), 4=Details (was 3), 5=Confirm (was 4). Minimal progress indicator now shows 5 numbered dots (01-02-03-04-05) with the same thin-line style. Slot picker fetches /api/slots?duration=<selected> on step entry (cached per duration), displays loading/error/empty states. Empty state shows message + "Request a time directly" skip button (sets skippedSlot=true → falls back to WhatsApp path). Slots grouped by date with Cinzel uppercase day headers + thin gold dividers; time slots in 2-3 column grid as borderless cards with bottom underline on hover; selected slot has gold border-bottom + bg tint. Selected slot chip + "skip" link shown below the grid. On final submit (step 5): if selectedSlot, POSTs to /api/slots/[selectedSlot.id] with full intake payload; shows success state with date/time confirmation card; if skipped (no slot), falls back to original WhatsApp flow (POST /api/bookings + openWhatsApp). Honeypot `website:''` field included in both paths. Booking success state has "back to start" reset button. All state (selectedSlot, skippedSlot, slotsLoading, slotsError, submitting, bookingSuccess, bookingError) managed via useState. Framer-motion AnimatePresence for step transitions preserved.

Session strategy: database. Pages: signIn/signOut/error/verifyRequest all → /account. Session callback attaches user.id to the session object for server-side use.
- Created /src/app/api/auth/[...nextauth]/route.ts — standard NextAuth route handler (`const handler = NextAuth(authOptions); export { handler as GET, handler as POST };`).
- Created /src/app/api/stripe/checkout/route.ts — POST endpoint with layered defense: (1) rate limit reusing RATE_LIMITS.bookings preset, (2) 4KB body cap, (3) honeypot silent-success for bots, (4) Zod validation (plan: 'monthly'|'yearly', optional email with .con/.cm typo guard, honeypot), (5) env-var guard returning 503 if STRIPE_PRICE_MONTHLY/YEARLY not set, (6) Stripe Checkout Session creation with mode=subscription, success_url=/account?status=success, cancel_url=/membership?status=cancelled, customer_email + metadata if provided, allow_promotion_codes enabled. Returns {url} for top-level browser navigation.
- Created /src/app/api/stripe/webhook/route.ts — POST handler that verifies Stripe signature using STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET + raw body (request.text()). Handles three events: (a) checkout.session.completed → upserts Membership with status=active, infers plan from price.recurring.interval, reads current_period_end from subscription.items.data[0] (Stripe API v22 moved this off Subscription to SubscriptionItem), links to NextAuth user by email if one exists; (b) customer.subscription.updated → syncs status/period/cancel flag; (c) customer.subscription.deleted → marks Membership expired (row preserved for history). All non-2xx returns trigger Stripe retry. Helper functions: asSubscription (type narrowing), mapStatus (active/trialing/past_due → active; canceled → expired; else → expired), getCurrentPeriodEnd (reads from items.data[0]), getInterval (reads price.recurring.interval), upsertMembership (lookup by subscriptionId OR customerId OR email, then update-or-create).
- Created /src/app/api/stripe/portal/route.ts — POST auth-gated endpoint that creates a Stripe Billing Portal session for the signed-in member. Returns {url} with return_url=/account?status=portal. 401 if no session, 404 if no membership or no stripeCustomerId on the membership row.
- Created /src/app/api/stripe/usage/route.ts — GET auth-gated endpoint returning the signed-in user's membership + recent bookings (last 12) + newsletter/drip preferences. Used by /account page for client-side refresh after Stripe redirects. 401 if no session.
- Created /src/app/api/preferences/route.ts — POST auth-gated endpoint for updating drip email preferences (prefSessions/prefBlog/prefDrip booleans) on the Newsletter row. Rate-limited (20/hour per IP), Zod-validated, upserts the Newsletter row if the user is signed in but never subscribed. Middleware has /api/preferences on the public-POST-API whitelist so bot UA + Origin check apply.
- Created /src/components/astrokalki/subscribe-button.tsx — client component for the /membership pricing page. Shows inline email field if no defaultEmail (signed-out user), hides it if signed in (with a "Use a different email" toggle). POSTs to /api/stripe/checkout with honeypot field, redirects window.location.href to the returned Stripe URL. Loading + error states.
- Created /src/components/astrokalki/sign-in-form.tsx — client component for the /account signed-out state. Fetches /api/auth/csrf, then POSTs to /api/auth/signin/email with email + csrfToken + callbackUrl=/account. Shows "Check your inbox" state after the request. Includes honeypot field.

Reads NextAuth session to: (a) pre-fill the SubscribeButton email when signed in, (b) render an "Already a member" panel linking to /account when the user has an active membership. Includes "What's inside" section explaining the four membership benefits (monthly sessions, recording archive, Pattern Atlas access, priority booking), a 6-question FAQ, OfferCatalog JSON-LD schema with INR pricing + ISO 8601 billing durations (P1M/P1Y), Breadcrumbs, and canonical + OpenGraph + Twitter metadata.

Membership status (plan/status/period-end/member-since grid + cancel-at-period warning or re-subscribe CTA), II. Subscription management (PortalLink, only if active), III. - Created /src/app/api/referrals/route.ts (rewritten): POST generates 8-char code from `ABCDEFGHJKLMNPQRSTUVWXYZ23456789` via crypto.getRandomValues, retry-checked for uniqueness (max 5 attempts), idempotent by email (returns existing code with `created:false` if email already a referrer). GET looks up by ?email=. Both rate-limited (POST 5/hour/IP, GET 30/min/IP). Zod-validated. Honeypot silent-success.
- Created /src/app/api/referrals/[code]/route.ts: GET public lookup by code, normalises to uppercase, validates format `/^[A-Z2-9]{8}$/` to reject obviously-wrong codes with 404 (avoids leaking code existence via format errors). Returns `{ valid, code, referrerName, uses, lastUsedAt }`. Rate-limited 30/min/IP.
- Created /src/app/api/referrals/track/route.ts: POST records a referral use. Idempotent — checks for existing (referralId, email) pair inside a transaction; if found, returns `{ tracked:true, idempotent:true }` with no increment. Otherwise creates ReferralUse + increments Referral.uses + sets lastUsedAt atomically. Zod-validated, honeypot-protected, rate-limited 10/hour/IP.
- Created /src/app/api/admin/referrals/route.ts: admin-gated GET, paginated list of all referrals with _count.referralUses. Supports ?sort=uses|recent|name. Returns `{ referrals, pagination, stats: { totalReferrals, totalUses, topReferrer } }`.
- Modified /src/app/api/admin/export/route.ts: added `type=referrals` branch. Emits one CSV row per ReferralUse joined to its Referral; referrals with 0 uses emit a single row with empty referred-* fields.
- Created /src/app/refer/page.tsx (server component): editorial referral hub. Hero "Refer a pattern. Not a product." → 3 numbered steps (01/02/03 in mono gold) → code generator form → stats lookup → 5-question FAQ. Breadcrumbs at top. SEO metadata + canonical URL. Full dark editorial design.
- Created /src/app/refer/ReferralForm.tsx (client component): react-hook-form + Zod. Two states: form (name + email) and success (code displayed in mono gold tracking-[0.15em] with Copy button using navigator.clipboard + execCommand fallback, WhatsApp share link `https://wa.me/?text=...` with editorial pre-filled message, uses + follow-ups-earned counters, "Generate another" reset). Honeypot field. Borderless inputs with bottom underline (matches booking.tsx + testimonials/submit).
- Created /src/app/refer/ReferralStats.tsx (client component): inline email lookup widget. Posts to GET /api/referrals?email=... and shows code in mono gold + use count + last-used date. Honest "no referral found" empty state.
- Created /src/app/admin/referrals/page.tsx (server component): admin dashboard with `dynamic='force-dynamic'`. Direct DB read. 4 StatCards (Total referrals, Total uses, Top referrer, Avg uses/code). Sort tabs (Most used / Recently used / By name — Link-based, server-rendered navigation). Table of all referrals (200 max) with columns: expand-arrow / Code (mono gold) / Referrer / Email / Uses (mono) / Last used / Created. Empty state. Export CSV link (opens /api/admin/export?type=referrals in new tab). Refresh link. mt-auto sticky footer.
- Created /src/app/admin/referrals/ReferralRow.tsx (client component): expandable table row. Clicking reveals ReferralUse history (each individual email + name + timestamp). Honest note when `uses > referralUses.length` explaining the booking-flow counter increment.
- Fixed one TS error in ReferralForm.tsx: removed dead code `{generated ? ... : ""}` after the early-return state branch (TS narrowed `generated` to `never` there).

    • `npx tsc --noEmit`: 0 errors in any of my files. (3 pre-existing errors in other agents' files: recordings/page.tsx missing modules, .next/types/validator.ts stale unsubscribe route.)

    • End-to-end smoke test (curl with browser UA + Origin):
        - GET /refer → 200, all sections render (hero, how-it-works, form, stats, FAQ), AstroKalki design system intact.
        - GET /admin/referrals without cookie → 307 redirect to /admin/login (middleware correctly gates).
        - GET /api/admin/referrals without cookie → 401 "Unauthorized — admin session required".
        - GET /api/admin/export?type=referrals without cookie → 401.
        - POST /api/referrals with valid payload → 201 `{ code:"MXDMN4RH", uses:0, created:true }`.
        - POST /api/referrals with same email → 200 `{ code:"MXDMN4RH", uses:0, created:false }` (idempotent).
        - GET /api/referrals?email=... → 200 with code + uses + createdAt.
        - GET /api/referrals/MXDMN4RH → 200 with code + referrerName + uses + lastUsedAt.
        - GET /api/referrals/NOTREAL1 → 404 "Invalid code format" (format rejection).
        - GET /api/referrals/bad → 404 "Invalid code format" (short codes rejected).
        - POST /api/referrals/track with new email → 201 `{ tracked:true, idempotent:false, uses:1 }`.
        - POST /api/referrals/track with same email → 200 `{ tracked:true, idempotent:true, uses:1 }` (no double-count).
        - GET /api/referrals/[code] after track → uses=1, lastUsedAt set.
        - Honeypot (website filled) → 200 fake success `{ message:"Subscribed successfully", subscribed:true, code:"THANKYOU0", uses:0 }`.
        - Zod validation (bad email) → 400 `email: Invalid email format`.
        - curl User-Agent (bot) → 403 "Request blocked" (middleware bot block fires before route handler).
        - With admin cookie: GET /api/admin/referrals → paginated list + stats (totalReferrals, totalUses, topReferrer).
        - With admin cookie: GET /api/admin/export?type=referrals → CSV with header row + one row per ReferralUse.
        - With admin cookie: GET /admin/referrals → 200, page contains "Admin · Referrals", "Referral programme", "Total referrals", "Total uses", "Top referrer", "Most used", "Showing", and the actual referral data (code + referrer name).
    • Test data cleaned up afterward (deleted test referral via Prisma — cascade removed ReferralUse rows).

Task: Pattern Atlas interactivity — add filtering by cluster/intensity, a side-by-side comparison view, and a "find your pattern" entry point that links the micro-reading quiz result to the relevant Atlas page.

Work Log:
- Read worklog.md end-to-end (UPGRADE-M1 schema prep, Task 7 Pattern Atlas history, M2-a+M4-b search work, M2-b testimonials, M3-c analytics, M2-e+M3-b Stripe/portal) to absorb design system, conventions, and existing Atlas structure. Confirmed Atlas is a single-file data export (`src/lib/content/patterns/atlas.ts`) with 11 patterns × 9 structured fields; NO cluster or intensity fields exist on the AtlasPattern type.
- Read `atlas.ts`, `patterns/atlas/page.tsx`, `patterns/atlas/[slug]/page.tsx`, `components/astrokalki/micro-reading.tsx`, `lib/i18n-context.tsx`, `lib/i18n.ts`, `lib/content/clusters.ts`, `lib/content/services.ts`, `components/astrokalki/breadcrumbs.tsx`, `app/layout.tsx`, `app/globals.css` to ground every design decision in the existing dark-editorial AstroKalki system (bg #050505, gold #c9a96e, text #f0eee9/#9a9a9a/#7a7a7a, Playfair Display for serif, Cinzel for labels via `.text-editorial` / `--font-cinzel` CSS var, Geist Mono for numbers, NO blue/indigo anywhere).

- CREATED `src/lib/content/patterns/micro-to-atlas.ts`:
  * The Atlas data is intentionally kept clean of taxonomy (so the source-of-truth file stays untouched by upstream agents). This file adds the classification layer.
  * Exports `AtlasCluster` ("Relationship" | "Emotional" | "Identity" | "Shadow") and `AtlasIntensity` ("Low" | "Medium" | "High") types, `ATLAS_CLUSTERS` / `ATLAS_INTENSITIES` ordered arrays.
  * Exports `ATLAS_META` record — cluster + intensity per Atlas slug. Classification was derived by reading each pattern's clinical description:
    - Relationship (4): the-rescuer, the-abandonment, the-chaser, the-avoider (patterns whose dominant expression is through the partner dynamic)
    - Emotional (2): the-emotional-caretaker, the-overthinker (patterns whose dominant expression is inner affect / emotional regulation)
    - Identity (4): the-performer, the-invisible-child, the-outsider, the-hyper-independent (patterns whose dominant expression is self-concept / role)
    - Shadow (1): the-self-sabotage (pattern whose dominant expression is hidden self-destruction)
  * Exports `getAtlasMeta(slug)` safe accessor returning "Uncategorised" / "Unknown" for unknown slugs (used by both the Explorer and the compare page).
  * Exports `microReadingToAtlasPattern(emotionalPattern, relationshipFrustration): string | null` — the function spec asked for. Strategy: each micro-reading emotional pattern (abandonment / control / people-pleasing / emotional-numbness / overthinking / self-doubt) maps to one or more Atlas patterns via the pattern's `relatedEssay` field (abandonment→abandonment-loop, control→control-loop, people-pleasing→people-pleasing, emotional-numbness→emotional-numbness, overthinking→overthinking, self-doubt→self-doubt). When multiple Atlas patterns share the same essay (e.g. abandonment-loop → both the-abandonment AND the-chaser), the relationship frustration ID is used as a tiebreaker (cant-leave → cling variant, same-fight → pursuit variant, etc.). Single-candidate essays (overthinking, self-doubt) map directly. Returns null only for unknown emotional patterns — caller links to /patterns/atlas hub.
  * Also exports `microReadingToAtlasPatternObject(...)` — convenience wrapper returning the resolved AtlasPattern object (used by the micro-reading CTA to render the pattern name in the link text).
  * Pure data + pure functions — runs on both server (compare page) and client (Explorer + micro-reading) without hydration mismatch.

- CREATED `src/app/patterns/atlas/AtlasExplorer.tsx` (client component, `'use client'`):
  * Replaces the static atlas grid on /patterns/atlas.
  * Filter bar (3 controls, all borderless Cinzel pills with gold underline-on-active):
    - Cluster pills: All / Relationship / Emotional / Identity / Shadow (animated underline scales 0→1 on active)
    - Intensity pills: All / Low / Medium / High (same underline pattern)
    - Search input: gold underline on focus, X clear button, 44px touch target
    - Compare toggle: pill that flips to "Cancel compare" with gold underline when active
  * Card grid: 1 col mobile / 2 col lg+, framer-motion `motion.div` + `layout` + `AnimatePresence mode="popLayout"` for smooth reflow on filter changes (enter from y:12, exit to y:-8, 0.35s ease-out). Each card shows: pattern number (mono), name (Playfair), tagline (Playfair italic), cluster tag (Cinzel gold/70), 3-dot intensity indicator (filled gold vs #2a2a2a dim + intensity label), read time (mono). Card click → /patterns/atlas/[slug].
  * Compare mode: when active, card click toggles selection (up to MAX_COMPARE=3); disabled state opacity-40 when at cap. Selected cards get gold border-l + bg tint + "Selected" pill. Floating action bar above grid shows "N of 3 selected · select X more" + "Compare selected" link (disabled until MIN_COMPARE=2 met) + Clear button. Compare-selected link routes to `/patterns/atlas/compare?patterns=slug1,slug2,slug3`.
  * Empty state: "No patterns match" + Reset filters CTA.
  * Footer: "Find your pattern" CTA → /#micro-reading (Cinzel gold underline link) + "The deeper essays" CTA → /patterns (replacing the duplicate footer that was in the old atlas hub).
  * All Cinzel labels use inline `style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-cinzel)' }}` since Tailwind has no built-in font-cinzel utility and we don't modify globals.css.

- CREATED `src/app/patterns/atlas/compare/CompareTable.tsx` (client component, `'use client'`):
  * Renders the side-by-side comparison table. Takes pre-resolved `CompareColumn[]` from the server page (one column per selected pattern, with pattern | null for not-found slugs).
  * Layout: CSS grid `minmax(140px, 180px) repeat(N, minmax(260px, 1fr))` — first column is row labels, rest are pattern columns. Horizontal scroll on small screens via `overflow-x-auto` wrapper.
  * Column headers: pattern number, cluster eyebrow, pattern name (Playfair, links to /patterns/atlas/[slug]), read-time mono. For not-found slugs: "Pattern not found" in italic grey.
  * Per-column controls (top-right of each column): ← reorder left, → reorder right, × remove. Both reorder and remove call `router.push` with the new comma-joined slug list so the URL stays shareable and the back button works.
  * Data rows (8 rows, in order): Cluster (Cinzel tag), Intensity (3 dots + Cinzel label), Core wound (Playfair italic quote, from pattern.tagline), Common trigger (prose, from symptoms[0]), How it shows up (prose, from howItShowsUp[0]), What it costs you (prose, from firstSentence(shadowSide)), The way through (prose, from lastSentence(conciseAnswer)), Related service (gold underline link to /services/[slug]).
  * Gold dividers between columns: `border-l border-[#c9a96e]/20` on every value cell. NO horizontal borders on cells — only `border-b border-white/[0.04]` between rows. This creates the editorial "gold rule" column dividers the spec called for.
  * Sentence helpers: `firstSentence(text)` regex-matches `^[^.!?]*[.!?]` for the cost row; `lastSentence(text)` splits on `(?<=[.!?])\s+` and takes the last for the way-through row.
  * "Add another pattern" link (Plus icon, gold underline) routes back to /patterns/atlas when cols.length < 3.
  * All Cinzel labels use inline style.

- CREATED `src/app/patterns/atlas/compare/page.tsx` (server component):
  * Reads `searchParams.patterns` (comma-separated slugs). `parseSlugs()` splits, trims, dedupes (preserving first-seen order), caps at 3 — exactly matching the AtlasExplorer MAX_COMPARE.
  * `buildColumns()` resolves each slug → CompareColumn (pattern | null, cluster, intensity, relatedServiceTitle, relatedServiceSlug) via `getAtlasPattern()` + `getAtlasMeta()` + `SERVICE_BY_SLUG`.
  * `generateMetadata()` produces a dynamic title: `Comparing The Rescuer Pattern vs The Abandonment Pattern — AstroKalki Pattern Atlas` (or with `vs X` for 3-pattern comparison). `robots: { index: false, follow: true }` — utility page, doesn't compete with the hub for SEO.
  * Emits `ItemList` JSON-LD schema with one ListItem per column, each pointing to a `DefinedTerm` item with the pattern's name + tagline + canonical URL. Helps AI search systems see the compared patterns as a structured related-items list.
  * Header: Breadcrumbs (Home → Pattern Atlas → Compare), Cinzel eyebrow "Pattern Atlas · Comparison", Playfair h1 "Side by side. Same architecture. Different wound.", copy paragraph that adapts based on whether enough patterns are selected.
  * Body: when ≥2 patterns → renders CompareTable with the resolved columns + a "Back to Atlas" link in the top-right. When <2 patterns → renders a NotEnoughPatterns empty state ("One more pattern to compare against." for 1-pattern, "Choose at least two patterns to begin." for 0) + "Open the Pattern Atlas" CTA. When 1 pattern is selected, also renders SuggestedPairings — 3 candidate patterns from DIFFERENT clusters than the selected one, each presented as a "Selected vs Candidate" link with a pre-built compare URL.

  * Added `atlasPattern` useMemo — resolves the user's primaryPattern (selectedPatterns[0] || "abandonment") + selectedFrustration to the most relevant Atlas pattern object. Recomputes only when those two inputs change.
  * In Step 5 (result reveal), inserted a NEW motion.div block between the result reveal and the fragment-note block. The new block fades in at delay 0.6s (after the result reveals at 0.3s, before the fragment note at 0.9s) — making it feel like the natural next step in the user journey: "see result → read more about it → eventually book the full decode".

Stage Summary:
- The Pattern Atlas is no longer static. Three new interactive capabilities ship:
  1. **Filtering**: by cluster (Relationship / Emotional / Identity / Shadow), by intensity (Low / Medium / High), and free-text search by name — all in borderless Cinzel-pills with animated gold underlines. Smooth card enter/exit via framer-motion AnimatePresence.

  3. **Find-your-pattern entry point**: the micro-reading quiz now ends with a prominent "Explore this pattern in the Atlas →" CTA — appearing at delay 0.6s in the result reveal (between the result fade-in at 0.3s and the existing "Book Full Decode" CTA at 0.9s). The CTA shows the resolved Atlas pattern name in Playfair italic so the user knows exactly which Atlas page they're being routed to. A new `microReadingToAtlasPattern(emotionalPattern, relationshipFrustration)` function maps each micro-reading result to the most relevant Atlas slug via the pattern's relatedEssay field, with relationship-frustration tiebreakers for ambiguous mappings. Falls back to the /patterns/atlas hub when no mapping can be derived.

All routes responsive (1-col mobile / 2-col lg+ grid on the Explorer; horizontal-scroll grid on the compare table for small screens).
- The Atlas is now a navigable knowledge layer rather than a static index. Users can browse by theme (cluster), find by intensity, compare two or three patterns side-by-side, and — most importantly — arrive at the Atlas naturally from the micro-reading quiz with a one-click path from "your pattern is X" → "read the full nine-field breakdown of X".

Task ID: M3-d
Agent: full-stack-developer
Task: Real-time availability WebSocket mini-service — build a socket.io mini-service in mini-services/availability/ that broadcasts AstroKalki's "in session / available / away" state + next booking slot, with a frontend live indicator that connects via the gateway.

Work Log:
- Read /home/z/my-project/worklog.md (full 1542-line history) — absorbed the AstroKalki design system (#050505 bg, #c9a96e gold, #4ade80 green, #f0eee9/#9a9a9a/#7a7a7a text, Cinzel labels, mono times), the M3-a slot-picker booking.tsx structure (5-step flow with slot picker as step 2), the UPGRADE-M1 socket.io@4.8.3 + socket.io-client@4.8.3 install, the existing public /api/slots?duration=60 endpoint (returns {slots:[{id,start,end,duration,status}]}), and the CRON_SECRET value in .env.
- Read examples/websocket/{server.ts,frontend.tsx} — confirmed the canonical gateway pattern: `path: "/"` on the server, `io("/?XTransformPort=<port>", ...)` on the client. Reused this pattern verbatim.

- CREATED /home/z/my-project/mini-services/availability/package.json (per task spec — exact contents: name, version 1.0.0, private, scripts.dev = "bun --hot index.ts", deps.socket.io ^4.8.3).

- CREATED /home/z/my-project/mini-services/availability/index.ts (~370 lines):
  * Loads .env from the project root (../../.env relative to script) at boot so CRON_SECRET is available — bun only auto-loads .env from the CWD, and the mini-service runs from mini-services/availability/, so a manual .env loader was required. Already-set process.env values take precedence (so explicit env on the command line wins).
  * Port 3003 HARDCODED — never read from env. (AVAILABILITY_PORT in .env is ignored.)
  * In-memory state: { status: 'available' | 'in-session' | 'away', nextSlot: ISO | null, currentSessionEnds: ISO | null }.
  * Default state: status='available', nextSlot = tomorrow 10:00 IST (computed as tomorrow 04:30 UTC), currentSessionEnds=null.
  * socket.io server with path: "/" (CRITICAL — required for Caddy XTransformPort routing), CORS via a function-based origin checker allowing http://localhost:3000, https://astrokalki.com, and https://preview-*.space-z.ai (regex). Connection logging to console.
  * On client connection: emits the current state immediately as a `state-change` event.
  * On state change (admin update or background refresh): broadcasts `state-change` to every connected client via io.emit.
  * Admin HTTP API at POST /admin/status (port 3003): CORS preflight + bearer-token auth (Authorization: Bearer <CRON_SECRET>); accepts { status?, nextSlot?, currentSessionEnds? } with strict validation (status enum check, ISO-date parse for nextSlot/currentSessionEnds, null allowed for nextSlot/currentSessionEnds, unknown fields rejected, empty update → 400, unauthorized → 401, CRON_SECRET unset → 503). 16KB body cap. Returns 200 with the new state.
  * GET /health (alias GET /) for ops/monitoring — returns { ok, service, state, clients }.
  * Background nextSlot sync: every 5 minutes (initial kick 5s after boot), fetches http://localhost:3000/api/slots?duration=60 (server-to-server, no XTransformPort needed). Takes slots[0].start as the new nextSlot. If the response is empty or the fetch fails, keeps the current nextSlot (silent fail — main app might be restarting). Only broadcasts if nextSlot actually changed.
  * CRITICAL FIX for socket.io path="/": when `path: "/"` is set, socket.io's request listener intercepts EVERY URL (including /admin/status and /health) and returns `{"code":0,"message":"Transport unknown"}` for anything that isn't an Engine.IO handshake. Solved by capturing socket.io's listener after attach, removing it, and re-adding a dispatcher that defers to socket.io ONLY for genuine Engine.IO handshakes (requests with `?EIO=` or `?transport=` query, or `Upgrade: websocket` header). Everything else is routed to my HTTP handler. Verified: /health, /admin/status, and socket.io connections all work simultaneously on the same port.
  * Query-string stripping for route matching — the gateway appends ?XTransformPort=3003 to every forwarded request, which would break exact-match URL comparisons. The HTTP handler now strips the query string before matching /health and /admin/status.
  * Graceful shutdown on SIGTERM/SIGINT (closes io, then httpServer, force-exits after 5s).

- CREATED /home/z/my-project/src/hooks/useAvailability.ts:
  * 'use client'. Exports useAvailability() returning { status, nextSlot, currentSessionEnds, connected }.
  * Connects via `io("/?XTransformPort=3003", { transports: ["websocket"], reconnection: true, reconnectionDelay: 1000, reconnectionAttempts: 5, timeout: 10000 })` — exact pattern from the task spec.
  * Subscribes to `connect`, `disconnect`, `state-change`, `connect_error`. Updates React state on each event.
  * Cleanup on unmount: removes every listener and disconnects the socket. SSR-safe (socket only created inside useEffect).
  * Defensive payload parsing: tolerates slightly-off state shapes (nextSlot/currentSessionEnds default to null if missing).
  * connect_error is silent (reconnection is automatic) — no console noise.

- CREATED /home/z/my-project/src/components/astrokalki/availability-indicator.tsx:
  * 'use client'. Imports useAvailability.
  * Returns null when disconnected OR when status is unknown — no broken UI.
  * Pulsing dot: 6×6px, color #4ade80 (available), #c9a96e (in-session), #7a7a7a (away). Uses Tailwind's `animate-pulse` class (2s ease-in-out, opacity 0.5↔1 — matches the task spec exactly).
  * Cinzel-uppercase 10px label: "Available now" / "In session" / "Away".
  * If status is 'in-session' or 'away' AND nextSlot exists: shows "· Next opening <relative time>" in mono — relative-time formatter renders "today, 10:00 AM" / "tomorrow, 10:00 AM" / "Wed, 10:00 AM" (≤6 days) / "12 Jun, 10:00 AM" (beyond), all in IST.
  * Two variants: `badge` (default, tight gap-2 spacing for nav bars) and `line` (gap-3, for section headers).
  * ARIA: role="status" + aria-live="polite" + descriptive aria-label so screen readers announce "AstroKalki is available now" (or with next opening).
  * Design system compliance: #050505 bg context, #c9a96e gold accent, #9a9a9a/#7a7a7a text, Cinzel labels, mono times, NO blue/indigo.

- MODIFIED /home/z/my-project/src/components/astrokalki/booking.tsx:
  * Added `import { AvailabilityIndicator } from "@/components/astrokalki/availability-indicator";` at the top.
  * Inserted a thin live-availability line at the very top of the booking section, just inside `<div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">` and above the step-0 emotional landing block. The line uses `<AvailabilityIndicator variant="line" />` inside a `flex items-center mb-10 sm:mb-14` wrapper.

      - POST /admin/status with bogus Bearer token → 401 Unauthorized

- How to start the mini-service:
    cd mini-services/availability
    bun install           # one-time, installs socket.io
    bun run dev           # runs `bun --hot index.ts`, listens on :3003
  The service prints "Availability service on :3003" on boot. It auto-loads CRON_SECRET from /home/z/my-project/.env (no manual env-file flag needed).

When the socket is disconnected (mini-service not running), the line renders nothing — the booking flow is unaffected.
- Connection pattern (CRITICAL): the frontend uses `io("/?XTransformPort=3003", { transports:["websocket"], reconnection:true, reconnectionAttempts:5, reconnectionDelay:1000 })`. The mini-service uses `path: "/"`. Caddy on port 81 forwards based on the XTransformPort query. Verified end-to-end via a bun socket.io-client test through the gateway.

The CRON_SECRET is shared with the main Next.js app's cron endpoints (same .env) so admins can drive the indicator from a server-side Next.js route, a cron job, or a future admin UI button.
- Sandbox note: the cloud sandbox kills background bun processes between bash calls, so the mini-service may need to be restarted manually before viewing the indicator live. The frontend gracefully renders nothing when the socket is disconnected, so the site is fully functional without the service running — the indicator simply appears once the service is started.

- Created /src/lib/security/playback-token.ts — `createPlaybackToken(recordingId, ttlMs)` and `verifyPlaybackToken(recordingId, token)`. Token format: `<base64url(hmac-sha256("${recordingId}:${expires}"))>.<expires>`. Uses ADMIN_SESSION_SECRET → falls back to ADMIN_PASSWORD (same secret as admin auth). 24h TTL. Web Crypto subtle.verify() for constant-time compare.
- Created /src/app/api/admin/recordings/route.ts (GET list + POST create). GET paginates (default 50, cap 100), supports ?bookingId= filter, includes booking {id,name,email,duration,price,status}. POST validates with Zod (title 2-200, duration 1-600 int, price 1-50, bookingId? nullable, audioUrl must start with /recordings/). Verifies booking exists before linking.
- Created /src/app/api/admin/recordings/[id]/route.ts (GET + PATCH + DELETE). GET returns single recording with full booking details. PATCH updates title/duration/price/bookingId (validates bookingId exists when set, supports null to unlink). DELETE removes DB row THEN deletes the audio file from disk via safeResolveAudioPath() (validates audioUrl starts with /recordings/ AND normalized path stays inside public/recordings/ — prevents path traversal). Returns {success, audioFileRemoved}.
- Created /src/app/api/admin/upload/route.ts — multipart/form-data upload of single `audio` field. 50MB cap enforced post-parse. Validates MIME type (audio/*) + extension (mp3/m4a/wav/ogg/flac/aac/weba). Saves to public/recordings/<uuid>.<ext> via crypto.randomUUID(). Returns {url, filename, originalName, size, mimeType}. The 4KB public-POST cap does NOT apply (admin routes bypass isPublicPostApi in middleware).
- Created /src/app/api/admin/bookings/route.ts — GET bookings search (?search=&limit=) for the recording manager's booking picker combobox. Searches across name OR email (case-insensitive contains), returns 7 fields per booking, capped at 50.
- Created /src/app/api/recordings/[id]/route.ts — public playback endpoint with signed-URL security. Looks up recording → verifies token (HMAC + expiry) → resolves file path defensively → streams via Node's createReadStream with Content-Type + Content-Range headers (HTTP 206 Partial Content for Range requests, 200 for full file). Supports byte-range seeking for HTML5 <audio> scrubbing.
- Created /src/app/api/recordings/[id]/token/route.ts — POST {email}. Validates email matches the booking's email. Rate-limited (10/hour per IP+email). 404 for unknown recording (no ID enumeration), 403 for no-booking recordings, 403 for email mismatch (same 403 — no email enumeration). Returns {token, expires, url, expiresInMs}.
- Created /src/app/admin/recordings/page.tsx — server component. Reads ?filter=all|attached|unattached. Stats tiles (total / total duration / unattached). Filter tabs as Link components (server-rendered navigation). Mounts RecordingManager + RecordingsTable. Sticky header with Back to /admin + Refresh. Sticky footer (mt-auto). Dark editorial design matching /admin/leads + /admin/testimonials.
- Created /src/app/admin/recordings/RecordingManager.tsx — client. Upload form with: file picker (drag-style dashed border), title (auto-fills from filename on first pick), duration presets (30/60/90/120) + custom number input, price (default ₹1,999), booking picker combobox (debounced search via /api/admin/bookings?search=, popover with results list, click to select, X to detach). Two-step submit: 1) POST file to /api/admin/upload via XHR with onprogress (so the admin sees bytes move for large 50MB files), 2) POST metadata to /api/admin/recordings. Progress bar with gold gradient. Done state with auto-close. Error states.
- Created /src/app/admin/recordings/RecordingPlayer.tsx — client. Minimal custom audio player for admin preview. Gold play/pause button (size-10/11 rounded-full), click-to-seek progress bar (gold gradient), time display (mono), volume slider, restart button. For attached recordings: fetches a signed token via the booking email so we exercise the real client path. For unattached (admin-only): falls back to direct /recordings/<file> URL since admin is already cookie-authed. NO default browser audio styling.
- Created /src/app/admin/recordings/RecordingsTable.tsx — client. Each recording as an expandable row: meta row (Attached/Unattached status, ID, created date), title + duration + price, booking reference (name + email + status, mailto link), action buttons (Play/Edit/Delete as text-link buttons with gold underline). Play expands inline RecordingPlayer. Edit expands inline form with same fields as upload (title/duration/price + booking picker). Delete confirms → DELETE → router.refresh(). Custom booking picker duplicated in the edit form (same debounced search).

On 403 (expired token after 24h), shows "Refresh access" button to re-issue token. Volume slider, click-to-seek progress bar, restart button.

Placeholder "e.g. MXDMN4RH". maxLength 32. Helper text: "If a friend shared an AstroKalki code with you, paste it here. They'll earn a free follow-up when you book." This lets users without a ?ref=CODE link still type a code manually, and lets users with one edit or clear it.
    6. Added a "Referral" line to the step 5 confirmation summary (between Focus areas and Investment) showing the code in mono gold when set — so the user sees it carried through to the final review.
    7. Updated the post-success reset handler to preserve referredBy (the URL still has ?ref=CODE, and the useEffect only runs on mount, so preserving the value lets a re-book in the same session keep the code).

- MODIFIED `src/app/api/admin/referrals/route.ts`: added optional `?email=` filter to the GET handler. Reads `email` from searchParams, trims + lowercases + caps at 254 chars, builds a Prisma `where` clause with `{ referrerEmail: { contains: emailFilter } }` (case-insensitive contains match — works for SQLite). The filter applies to the paginated list + the row count, but NOT to the global stats (totalReferrals, totalUses, topReferrer) — those remain programme-wide so the publisher still sees overall totals while filtering. Updated the JSDoc comment to document the new param. The filter is used by future admin UI search affordances (e.g. "find a referrer by email fragment").

- CREATED /src/app/api/admin/recordings/upload/route.ts (~190 lines) — the spec'd upload endpoint path. Handler: POST multipart/form-data with single `audio` field. Validates MIME (audio/* prefix) + extension (.mp3/.m4a/.wav/.ogg/.oga/.weba/.flac/.aac). 50MB hard cap enforced after formData parse (returns 413 with size info). MIME→extension fallback map for clients that send generic audio/* without a usable filename. Creates public/recordings/ via fs.mkdir({recursive:true}) if missing. Writes to public/recordings/<uuid>.<ext> via Buffer.from(await file.arrayBuffer()) + fs.writeFile. Returns { url:"/recordings/<uuid>.<ext>", filename, originalName, size, mimeType } with 201 status. Path-traversal-safe (filename is server-generated UUID, never derived from client input). Errors: 400 missing field / wrong field type / empty file / invalid multipart, 413 too large, 415 unsupported type, 500 storage failure.

- DELETED /src/app/api/admin/upload/route.ts and removed the now-empty /api/admin/upload/ directory — the old non-spec'd path. All references to it (in RecordingManager.tsx and a comment in /api/admin/recordings/route.ts) were updated.

Part A — preference-aware cron routes:
- MODIFIED /src/app/api/cron/drip/route.ts:
  * Day +2 candidate query: added `prefDrip: true` to the WHERE clause (alongside `optedOut: false`). Subscribers who muted the nurture sequence in the preference center will no longer receive Day +2 emails.
  * Day +5 candidate query: same `prefDrip: true` addition.
  * Added explanatory comments above both queries documenting why the preference gate matters (the /unsubscribe preference center lets subscribers mute just the nurture sequence without losing session/blog emails).
- MODIFIED /src/app/api/cron/birthday/route.ts:
  * Newsletter-candidates query: added `prefSessions: true` to the WHERE clause. Birthday emails are session-related (they invite the recipient to book their annual reading), so they respect the session-emails preference.
  * Micro-reading recipients loop: added a `record?.prefSessions === false` skip check (alongside the existing `record?.optedOut` check). New rows created below default to prefSessions=true (schema default), so first-time micro-reading recipients still receive the birthday email — only existing subscribers who explicitly muted session emails are skipped.

  * Created a test row with prefDrip=false, dripStage=0, lastDripAt=72h ago (qualifies for Day+2 by date). Confirmed it appears in the "without filter" query but NOT in the "with prefDrip=true filter" query. PASS.

  * Required-field labels now show a visible gold asterisk (`*`) with `aria-hidden="true"` so sighted users see the convention and screen readers don't double-announce.
  * All six inputs + the message textarea + the referredBy input now carry `aria-invalid={!!bookingError || undefined}` so when a form-level error is present, screen readers announce "invalid entry" on focus.
  * All inputs now carry `aria-describedby="booking-error"` (conditionally rendered when bookingError is present) linking each input to the live error message.
  * The bookingError `<p>` now has `id="booking-error"`, `role="alert"` (was already there), and `aria-live="assertive"` so screen readers announce the error immediately when it appears.

  * Email input now has `aria-describedby="micro-reading-email-hint"` linking it to the hint paragraph below (which got `id="micro-reading-email-hint"`). Screen readers now announce the "We respect your inbox. Unsubscribe anytime." hint on focus.
  * Email input now has `aria-invalid={email.length > 0 && !email.includes("@") ? true : undefined}` — marks the field invalid only when the user has typed something that clearly isn't an email (no @). Avoids the trap of marking the field invalid on every keystroke.
  * Reveal button now has a descriptive `aria-label`: `${t("microReading.reveal")} — submit your email to reveal your micro-reading`.

"page" : undefined}` to each `<Link>`, where `isActive = pathname === item.href || (item.href !== "/" && pathname.startsWith(item.href + "/"))`. The active link is also visually highlighted in gold (#c9a96e) instead of the muted gray (#7a7a7a) — both sighted and screen-reader users can identify the current page. Add a Next.js REST proxy at `/api/admin/availability`, an admin control page at `/admin/availability` (matching the /admin/leads design), and surface `<AvailabilityIndicator />` subtly in the hero CTA row.
